                        <span class="_1-h1 _3q_m" title="It's Wikipedia's 19th birthday! 🎉

To celebrate #WikipediaDay this year, we're recognizing our awesome global community of volunteers who help collect sources, verify info, and edit articles. Have you thanked a Wikipedian today? Give a ❤️ below to show your support.">
                         It's Wikipedia's 19th birthday! 🎉

To celebrate #WikipediaDay this year, we're recognizing our awesome global community of volunteers who help collect sources, verify info, and edit articles. Have you thanked a Wikipedian today? Give a ❤️ below to show your support.
                        </span>

                        <div class="_5pbx userContent _3576" data-ft='{"tn":"K"}' data-testid="post_message">
                         <p>
                          "As a collection, it is an exhaustive expression of what it is to be human, all set against a myriad of African backdrops."⁣ —
                          <a class="profileLink" href="https://www.facebook.com/wikilovesafrica/?fref=mentions">
                           Wiki Loves Africa
                          </a>
                          jury facilitator, Isla Haddow-Flood.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Over 1,140 photographers submitted 8,319 images to this year's competition. See the winners.
                          <span class="_5mfr">
                           <span class="_6qdm" style='height: 16px; width: 16px; font-size: 16px; background-image: url("https://static.xx.fbcdn.net/images/emoji.php/v9/tde/1/16/1f4f8.png")'>
                            📸
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </p>
